			add_ideas = FEA_bill_of_rights_pvda
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = FEA_ldp_policies
			}
			remove_ideas = FEA_ldp_policies_idea2
			remove_ideas = FEA_fair_labor_act_ldp_idea3
			remove_ideas = FEA_fair_deal
			add_ideas = FEA_bill_of_rights_ldp
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = FEA_fhp_policies
			}
			remove_ideas = FEA_fhp_policies_idea3
			remove_ideas = FEA_domestic_policies
			remove_ideas = FEA_minimum_wage_fhp
			add_ideas = FEA_bill_of_rights_fhp
		}
		else = {
			remove_ideas = FEA_fnv_policies_idea2
			remove_ideas = FEA_domestic_policies
			remove_ideas = FEA_minimum_wage_fnv
			remove_ideas = FEA_strategic_fuel_reserves
			add_ideas = FEA_bill_of_rights_fhp
		}
